       $(function () {
                 
                 // Set Cookie that is valid for a day as soon as the user closes the overlay
                 $('.eb_mobilebanner .eb_close-overlay').on('click', function() {
                     var tExpirationDate= new Date();
                     tExpirationDate.setTime(tExpirationDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24);
                     $.cookie('eb_mobilebanner', 'gesetzt', {
                         expires: tExpirationDate
                     });
                     
                     $('.eb_mobilebanner').detach();
                     
                     $(window).trigger('resize');
                 });
             });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function () {
                 
                 // Set Cookie that is valid for a day as soon as the user closes the overlay
                 $('.eb_mobilebanner .eb_close-overlay').on('click', function() {
                     var tExpirationDate= new Date();
                     tExpirationDate.setTime(tExpirationDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24);
                     $.cookie('eb_mobilebanner', 'gesetzt', {
                         expires: tExpirationDate
                     });
                     
                     $('.eb_mobilebanner').detach();
                     
                     $(window).trigger('resize');
                 });
             });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function () {
                 
                 // Set Cookie that is valid for a day as soon as the user closes the overlay
                 $('.eb_mobilebanner .eb_close-overlay').on('click', function() {
                     var tExpirationDate= new Date();
                     tExpirationDate.setTime(tExpirationDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24);
                     $.cookie('eb_mobilebanner', 'gesetzt', {
                         expires: tExpirationDate
                     });
                     
                     $('.eb_mobilebanner').detach();
                     
                     $(window).trigger('resize');
                 });
             });
      </script>

           <h4 id="ctl19_ctl01_ctl51_paTitel">
            Telefonischer Kontakt
           </h4>
           <div class="notfallnummern" id="ctl19_ctl01_ctl51_paTextContainer">
            <div class="form-group">
             <div class="inhalt" id="ctl19_ctl01_ctl51_paTextInhalt">
              <p>
               <strong>
                Telefonservice
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               0711 90050-2900
              </p>
              <p>
               Montag - Freitag: 06:00-22:00 Uhr
               <br/>
               Samstag und Sonntag: 09:00-16:00 Uhr
               <br/>
               Wenn an der Deutschen Börse gehandelt wird, auch an Feiertagen von 08:00-22:00 Uhr
              </p>
              <p>
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
                Telefonberatung
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               0711 90050-3500
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               Montag - Mittwoch: 08:00-16:00 Uhr
               <br/>
               Donnerstag: 08:00-17:30 Uhr

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function () {
                 
                 // Set Cookie that is valid for a day as soon as the user closes the overlay
                 $('.eb_mobilebanner .eb_close-overlay').on('click', function() {
                     var tExpirationDate= new Date();
                     tExpirationDate.setTime(tExpirationDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24);
                     $.cookie('eb_mobilebanner', 'gesetzt', {
                         expires: tExpirationDate
                     });
                     
                     $('.eb_mobilebanner').detach();
                     
                     $(window).trigger('resize');
                 });
             });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function () {
                 
                 // Set Cookie that is valid for a day as soon as the user closes the overlay
                 $('.eb_mobilebanner .eb_close-overlay').on('click', function() {
                     var tExpirationDate= new Date();
                     tExpirationDate.setTime(tExpirationDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24);
                     $.cookie('eb_mobilebanner', 'gesetzt', {
                         expires: tExpirationDate
                     });
                     
                     $('.eb_mobilebanner').detach();
                     
                     $(window).trigger('resize');
                 });
             });
      </script>
